<userid>110753367084927927004< /userid><username>Bob Thompson<//username>< Date>
1617210966862< /Date>
< rating>
4</rating>
< review>
We got a brief respite from the rain, as sun, blue skies and fluffy white clouds appeared, propelling us out of the house, for a drive down to the harbor.

When we arrived, a huge gray cloud obscured the sun, making a chilly breeze even colder.  Then, like magic, the sun freed itself, bringing with it welcoming bright light and a warm embrace.  There are lots of nice yachts & smaller boats  slipped in colorful rows within the harbor, plus 2 sportfishing companies operate here: Helgren's Landing and Chubasco 2 Sportfishing.

There are many restaurants in the harbor area too, accompanied by ample parking in the vicinity.  A large cluster of these dining places are grouped together at Oceanside Harbor Village. They include: Joe's Crab Shack, Rockin' Baja Lobster, Harbor Fish & Chips, Lighthouse Oyster Bar & Grill, & Tony's Sports Bar & Grill, plus Nana & Pop Pop's Ice Cream & Sweet Shop. These are accessed by veering left at the Y, upon driving downhill into the Oceanside Harbor area.  This touristy spot is called Oceanside Harbor Village.  You can also get to Oceanside Harbor Beach, a kid friendly, wide sandy beach, by heading this direction.

If you veer right at the Y, you'll have access to Helgren's Sportfishing, Oceanside Broiler Restaurant, plus a small reel repair & tackle shop.  This area is Oceanside Harbor.  The road in this direction dead-ends at the opening to the harbor, where ships enter and exit a narrow jetty-protected channel, into the open ocean.< /review>

< Text>
I always enjoyed being in Oceanside Harbor when out here visiting family in the summer. Usually saw some sea lions while paddling my sea kayak from South Harbor out through the jetties and offshore. There were always sea lions on the Red OC buoy going out too. And on occasion you got to see some interesting Navy training using various amphibious vehicles.< /Text>

< review>
Oceanside Harbor has more than just slips for your boat. Boasting nearly two miles of paved walkways, plenty of benches and tables to sit and eat, and ample parking are a few other perks. A sprinkling of hotels are located with amazing views and the restaurants generally focus on delicious seafood fare.<//review>

< Name>
M. Muhls</Name>
<date>1540441573558<//date><rate>3<//rate>< text>
Local parking is ok, there is a free parking lot we’re local fisher men, surfers and adrenaline enthusiast skateboard or just hang out and listen to music. I did notice a few RVs which made me wonder if you can camp here in this free lot. Other than that it is your basic lot. It has a occasional train passing by and someone asking for change. We have been paring here for years and have never had any problems. Get there early to get a good spot, especially in the summer months. If you arrive after 8am during that time all lots will be full. It’s the price you pay for living in So Cal. Watch out for sting rays! We got stung, it’s not fun! Have respect for nature!!<//text>

It’s the one that you stop at only because it’s on the way or is the most convenient. The environment is dirty and the inside bottom of the cup is a thick layer of unmixed powder.

< Text>
I was at this Westfield mall in Escondido last Wednesday getting a car battery check-up.As we all know getting work done on your car can take hours but my wife and I had recently been to the new Elixir Expresso & Wine Bar in La Jolla and we found out they also have a location in this center.As it turned out Elixir was on the bottom level only a short walk from the store where I dropped my car off.A young lady named Jackie greeted me very happily and took my order for a latte and a crepe.I know their coffee is very good because they use our favorite Caffe Calabria roasted coffee beans at all their locations and their long slim crepes are very good value.Thanks to Ty for making my superb latte and the delicious crepe.And thank the stars I found some place decent to have lunch at because my car wasn't ready for another 3 hours.....and for around $13 with a tip it was great value.Friendly staff,great service,terrific food and beverages and a handy location away from the food court makes this business a winner.</Text>

<Text>Clean park and the manager couldn't be any nicer, he spent an hour and a half in the pouring rain and ankle deep water to help me get parked. This was when California was being hit by three major storms one after the other. He was also able to transfer us over here the same day when the park in Davis didn't have our spot available.

We have a triple slide 30ft fifth wheel and at least with the spots available now this was the only one we could fit in. So keep that in mind if you have a large rig, you may not fit. The manager should be able to let you know. He was excellent at getting me into the spot as I was alone and therfore should be able to tell you what would it wouldn't fit.

I'm very happy right now but I've just arrived but I'm impressed with the somewhat new manager from what I understand from other reviews. It sounds like he really cleaned it up. Probably the nicest manager I've dealt with in four years of full-timing and we've been to a lot of parks.<//Text>< Pictures>

<userid>116688653851063668748<//userid><user_name>D Taylor<//user_name><rating>5</rating><gmap_id>0x808514396c083523:0x63f21e9564b30b2f<//gmap_id><Time>1532118495093< /Time>< text>
Actually, I rate it BOTH a 5 star and a 1 star. THE GOOD: Very professionally run. Full range of facilities including pool, spa and separate fitness and rec centers, laundry room, 48 cable channels, showers, dog friendly (though I did not see an actual dog run), storage units and one of the best recycling/garbage areas I've ever come across. Park is clean, well maintained, properly paved, flat spaces, tree lined. So, why also a 1 star? THE BAD: With more than 400 spaces, there is always someone nearby idling a diesel engine or banging about. With 400 spaces, the showers were so far away, we used our own tiny, mini-motorhome shower rather than hike to theirs. The tree-lined park blocked my satellite service to DirecTV (space 15) so we used their cable service but it was of very poor signal (would be IMPOSSIBLE to watch a football or baseball game; okay for the evening news). Airport and train noise is not horrible but is definitely audible. Because it is so large, it felt like being in a condo complex (kinda tight between the units).</text>

< review>
Nice Golf course. A little dated. It probably was a private country at one time mabye 30 years ago. Great scenery of the mountains. We played on Jan 17 2021. Played in afternoon. It was only $30 with a cart. Needs little upgrading and more maintenance but has potential and we had a great time. It's worth coming when no one is here. It's a good value. I would come again. Enjoy!</review>

<Name>David Cho< /Name>< Review>
Not bad for the price, especially if you used Groupon like I did. First 18 of the year for me and just the 2nd golf experience ever for my GF so we didn’t want to pay a lot or deal with crowds and this place fit the bill. Yes, there are issues. Greens are overgrown and slow, no bar or restaurant to speak of and they lack restrooms on the back nine. I guess a flood created some issues and could not re-open fully. Otherwise the fairways were in decent shape and we had the privacy we were looking for.

Pro tip: make sure to take your own beer, water and snacks. They do offer up some sandwiches and snacks in pro shop but not sure when they were made.</Review>

This is definitely not a place to go if you can golf.... At least not on the weekend.

You had to wait every shot. Tons of beginners just learning to play and not familiar with etiquette.

The conditions are terrible and they have a ton of temporary holes because of damage from over a year ago!! I'm not sure what's taking so long to make the repairs. I guess they don't care because people are still coming out.

They are the cheapest price in the valley.

The staff are all friendly.</text>

< Review>
This is not a nature friendly complex, the gardeners keep trimming the trees, bushes, bougainvilliers so much that there are no leaves, no flowers left. They should know that in the summer green keeps the air fresher but no they have to chop down everything and to make it worse they do it all morning starting at 7 so it' impossible to sleep. Phase 4 is a ;little bit more quiet but they cut everything just the asme as in phase 3 (the one on the west handside of Farrell). I saw a bunch of dead bees by the pool and it smelt of chemical so I believe they spray something to kill the bees, some of them were not dead and if I hadn't been careful I could have stepped on one of them and got stung. I was thinking of buying a condo at East Mesquite, I won't because I'd be arguing with landscaping management all the time. The HOAs could be twice as cheap if they saved on the numbers of hours devoted to cutting trees that don't need to or mowing grass that is way too short. However I have to concede that it is a well maintained and overall pleasant property, but it coulod be more pleasant if the bougainvilliers around the pool were left intact instead of being trimmed to the point that they don't allow for privacy.<//Review>

<GmapID>0x80d959c9cc055241:0xb9186a160ec5c5d7<//GmapID>< Text>
My barista was so pleasant! And, she knows her drinks and how their made. I stopped in on March 6, 2021 and ordered an iced caramel macchiato made with almond milk , with 2 extra pumps of simple syrup and 1 extra of caramel. She explained the caramel is drizzled on top of the drink and asked if I’d rather have the extra put in the drink itself and also that vanilla syrup is used, not simple syrup and asked if I’d like maybe an extra pump of the syrup instead of the caramel. I went with her suggestion : 2 pumps of vanilla syrup, no extra caramel and it was very, very, good! Why had no other Starbucks barista corrected me about the syrup??!! A small thing but I appreciated the clarification. This Resturant is on the smallish side but clean and comfy. Nice selection of pastries, sandwiches, protein packs, cups for sale, etc. I also liked the location.< /Text>

<review>Solid Starbucks 'experience' here. One of the biggest differentiating factors between Starbucks locations is the physical space they occupy, so I'll comment on that here as everything else about this store is essentially standard across the chain. This location is medium-sized as they go; there's some window counter space with seating and a handful of indoor tables, and in my experience has not been overly crowded with finding a spot to sit down. Of course this will vary depending on the time of day, etc. but I would not characterize this location as exceptionally busy. There are also several outdoor tables which is always a nice option to have in sunny San Diego.</review><Gmap_id>0x80d959c9cc055241:0xb9186a160ec5c5d7</Gmap_id><UserId.>109102764303771329043</UserId.><time>1554859160753< /time>< response>

I had such a great experience with Paola’s Flowers. My uncle passed away and I was trying to figure out ordering flowers for a small service. I looked at their website, and liked what I saw. I think they are in charge of too many tables because you don't see them really more than two to four times in the entire visit. It can take a few minutes to flag them down if you need something. Usually I have to flag them down for a  refill on my beverage.  I had special promotional gift cards to use along with a regular gift card. They are supposed to be able to be scanned on the tablet device, but each time it hasn't worked. I then had to wait to flag them down, in which they have to flag their manager down to take care of it. Each time, the manager has had issues getting the promotional gift cards to work.  Thankfully the manager will get it all to work, but it all takes time. I might spend about forty-five minutes from ordering to finishing eating, but then I spend an additional forty-five minutes to try and get the payment figured out.  The food is amazing and very good. Not the best Chili's I've been to. Staff is generally very pleasant, but I find that they're only attentive to your table up until your main course arrives. At that point they are no where to be found except for their initial "How is everything?" at the two minute mark, most likely with food in your mouth, and barely giving you time to swallow and respond before wondering off to another table. The last meal I got there, took much longer than tables that were seated way after myself, the food came out lukewarm to cold, and then we were stuck there for days waiting to pay our tab and leave. Honestly only good to go during Happy Hours for cheap apps and/or endless chips.< /review>

<gmap_id>0x8090504ec98781ad:0x776a16d2dc8e386c</gmap_id>< Time>
1494638406273<//Time>
< Pics>
None<//Pics>
< text>
Never will I step foot inside another Chilis establishment due to my experience at the Chilis in Modesto, CA.

I recently moved to the Modesto area from Florida and decided to grab some food and drinks with my sister.

We ordered drinks and as expected the server asked for our IDs, we handed her our Florida issued drivers licenses (we have not been here long enough to obtain CA IDs). What I did not expect was for her to walk away with them with no explanation. After about 5-10 mins, a different person approached us with our IDs and introduced herself as Heather, the manager, and stated that they were unable to accept our IDs and proceeded to explain her reasons:
1.	One of the IDs was cracked. She bends the ID as she attempts to show the "crack" that wasn't there.
2.	One of our IDs had a star and the other did not. SN: Florida licenses have changed within the past few years and each of ours were issued at different times. One is more current than the other. But both are VALID state issued IDs. The issue date is clearly printed on the front of the ID.
3.	It did not match the Florida ID in their "book". As explained in the 2nd reason, the state of Florida has more than one ID type therefore if we're going to be matching IDs to a "book" you need to have all IDs for each state.
At no point during this interaction did the manager offer to accommodate us for the inconvenience and her apology was artificial and insincere. Not willing to tolerate any further disrespect and unwarranted embarrassment we immediately left.

Since the time of the interaction I have spoken with Heather again via phone as well as Ken, the general manager, to understand their procedures and how they could allow potential customers to walk away upset, when we had done nothing wrong.

The attempt to give them an opportunity to at least genuinely and sincerely apologize and or offer a reasonable explanation lead nowhere with no attempt at a resolution on their part. I am infuriated at how poorly this situation was handled and will advise anyone I know against going to any Chilis establishment. Chilis Executives - please better train your management and staff on how to properly and respectfully handle interactions with customers.</text>

< Text>
Okay Chili's.. Look. I love eating here, I love the Tropical Sunrise Margaritas and Priscilla (sp?) was a great server last night. We were not in her section, but she took us on anyways. It was about 9:00 last night 11/11/14. We went because, for one, we have been loyal customers for like ever now and absolutely love our experience every time. Two, it was Veterans Day so it was a win win for us. Great food, my fiance got his meal for free. Thank you! So. Anyways.. Let's get to the point. Give Priscilla a raise or something, she was awesome. Also that one guy that I think is a manager in that striped shirt, he was cool too. HOWEVER, like I have already said, I have been a loyal customer for a long time. I order the same thing, without fail, every single time I go in. I order a Tropical Sunrise Margarita, Triple Dipper and a Mushroom Swiss Burger. I can count on getting the same thing every time. I've had Chili's all the way from Modesto, Ca to Denver, Co. You guys are reliable, fast, friendly, courteous, etc. Well, after hundreds or dollars spent, I go in last night to spend another $50 bucks and order the Mushroom Swiss Burger. Oh but wait, THERE ARE NO MORE MUSHROOMS. WHAT!? Can you imagine my surprise? I had my order ready to go even before we got seated. Even before I even got off of work. I had to sit there and stare at the menu for what felt like forever just to figure out a way to cope with the loss of mushrooms. I am not someone to mix things up, but last night I was really thrown for a loop. There are literally no decent Mushroom Swiss Burgers anywhere in my area. Oh my Jesus. How do you just not have ANY mushrooms? For a brief moment, I was lost and confused. I felt like the whole world had come to a stop awaiting my decision. The fate of the world rest upon my shoulders and I had been so unprepared to do something else. I had no plan B. There was never a thought in my mind that I would have to do something different, to take a different route and change my path forever. No mushrooms, you say? Fine, I will bring my own next time. Please tell me that you still have Swiss cheese. Oh, also, DO NOT EVER GET RID OF THE TROPICAL SUNRISE MARGARITA! That will literally send me over the edge. Thank you.<//Text>
